# Allows you to create your own dynamic keys
# to be called in localization.
# defined_text -> this is it, we're defining the text
# text -> a discrete entry that can be picked to display in loc.
# trigger -> determines if a text entry will be picked or not.
# (The triggers need to be valid for the scope the key is called in
# (eg Root or From.From).)
# localization_key -> points to the localization key
# that'll be used if trigger passes
defined_text = {
	# Country
	name = GetRaceName
	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_griffon_race = yes
		}
		localization_key = griffon_race_type

defined_text = {
	# Country
	name = GetHand
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_griffon_race = yes
				is_harpy_race = yes
				is_hippogriff_race = yes
			}
		}
		localization_key = hand_talon
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_pony_race = yes
				is_deer_race = yes
				is_changeling_race = yes
				is_yak_race = yes
				is_buffalo_race = yes
				is_camel_race = yes
				is_donkey_race = yes
				is_giraffe_race = yes
				is_horse_race = yes
				is_kirin_race = yes
				is_llama_race = yes
				is_zebra_race = yes
			}
		}
		localization_key = hand_hoof
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_diamond_dog_race = yes
				is_polar_race = yes
				is_cat_race = yes
			}
		}
		localization_key = hand_paw
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_centaur_race = yes
				is_minotaur_race = yes
				is_gargoyle_race = yes
				is_yeti_race = yes
			}
		}
		localization_key = hand_hand
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_generic_race = yes
		}
		localization_key = hand_appendage
	}
}
